									</p><div class="date">1212 DD, YYYY</div></div><div class="content-card tech"><span class="tag">TECH</span><h3><a href="https://www.theverge.com/news/704606/subnautica-2-delay-krafton-unknown-worlds-bonus">Krafton slams ex-Subnautica 2 execs ‚Äî who now say they‚Äôre suing</a></h3><p class="desc">
											

						
&lt;figure&gt;

&lt;img alt=&quot;&quot; data-caption=&quot;&quot; data-portal-copyright=&quot;Image: Unknown Worlds&quot; data-has-syndication-rights=&quot;1&quot; src=&quot;https://platform.theverge.com/wp-content/uploads/sites/2/2025/07/Subnautica_2_Early_Access_Key_Art.png?quality=90&amp;#038;strip=all&amp;#038;crop=0,0,100,100&quot; /&gt;
	&lt;figcaption&gt;
		&lt;/figcaption&gt;
&lt;/figure&gt;
&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;&lt;em&gt;Subnautica 2 &lt;/em&gt;has been at the center of a contentious debate between leadership at its developer Unknown Worlds and the game‚Äôs publisher, Krafton Games. At stake is a $250 million payout, promised to Unknown Worlds if the studio hit certain revenue targets by the end of this year. But a company shakeup and the subsequent delay of &lt;em&gt;Subnautica 2 &lt;/em&gt;has rocked the studio and potentially imperiled the promised payout, and now one of Unknown World‚Äôs fired founders says they‚Äôre suing.&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;On July 2nd, Krafton announced that Steve Papoutsis, CEO of &lt;em&gt;The Callisto Protocol&lt;/em&gt; developer Striking Distance Studios &lt;a href=&quot;https://krafton.com/en/news/press/krafton-announces-gaming-industry-veteran-steve-papoutsis-as-new-ceo-of-unknown-worlds/&quot;&gt;would be taking over as the CEO of Unknown Worlds&lt;/a&gt;, replacing the current leadership of Ted Gill, Charlie Cleveland, and Max McGuire with immediate effect.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;The following week, on July 9th, Unknown Worlds announced that &lt;a href=&quot;https://unknownworlds.com/en/news/subnautica-2-coming-2026&quot;&gt;early access for &lt;em&gt;Subnautica 2&lt;/em&gt; would be delayed to 2026&lt;/a&gt;. According to the announcement, &lt;em&gt;Subnautica 2&lt;/em&gt; was in good shape, but closed testing revealed ‚Äúsome insight that there are a few areas where we needed to improve before launching the first version of&lt;em&gt; Subnautica 2&lt;/em&gt; to the world.‚Äù&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;That same day, &lt;em&gt;Bloomberg&lt;/em&gt;‚Äôs Jason Schreier &lt;a href=&quot;https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2025-07-09/krafton-delays-subnautica-2-game-ahead-of-250-million-payout&quot;&gt;reported that&lt;/a&gt; this delay was against the wishes of Unknown Worlds‚Äô former leadership and that there were serious financial implications for this delay. According to Schreier‚Äôs report, when Krafton purchased Unknown Worlds, in 2021 it promised a $250 million bonus to the studio if it hit revenue targets by the end of 2025. Schreier‚Äôs reporting also indicated that the bonus was planned to be shared among the studio‚Äôs roughly 100 employees with some being promised bonuses in the seven figures.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;With &lt;em&gt;Subnautica 2&lt;/em&gt;‚Äôs delay, those revenue targets will likely not be hit, and those bonuses not paid out. In a statement to &lt;em&gt;Bloomberg&lt;/em&gt;, Krafton said the delay was only to improve &lt;em&gt;Subnautica 2&lt;/em&gt;‚Äôs quality, and it‚Äôs possible to envision a situation where &lt;a href=&quot;https://www.theverge.com/news/703373/krafton-delay-subnautica-2-250-million-bonus&quot;&gt;Krafton delayed the game in order to get out of paying out the bonus&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;However, Krafton has issued a new statement that seemingly throws cold water over this interpretation. The statement says that Krafton had ‚Äúallocated approximately 90% of the up to $250 million earn-out compensation to the three former executives‚Äù with the ‚Äúexpectation‚Äù that the executives would ‚Äúdemonstrate leadership and active involvement in the development of &lt;em&gt;Subnautica 2&lt;/em&gt;.‚Äù The statement then accuses the ousted leadership of essentially abandoning development on the game while affirming ‚Äúfair and equitable compensation for all remaining Unknown Worlds employees.‚Äù&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;Later on Thursday, Unknown Worlds co-founder &lpar;and¬†&lt;em&gt;Subnautica&lt;/em&gt;¬†director&rpar; Charlie Cleveland responded to these accusations by saying he‚Äôs filed a lawsuit. ‚ÄúAs for the earnout, the idea that Max, Ted and I wanted to keep it all for ourselves is totally untrue,‚Äù &lt;a href=&quot;https://www.charliecleveland.com/lawsuit/&quot;&gt;he writes&lt;/a&gt;. ‚ÄúHistorically we‚Äôve always shared our profits with the team and did the same when we sold the studio.‚Äù&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;We‚Äôve asked for a copy of the legal complaint.&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;Here are Krafton and Cleveland‚Äôs statements in full. You can also see them &lt;a href=&quot;https://www.krafton.com/en/&quot;&gt;on Krafton‚Äôs website&lt;/a&gt; and &lt;a href=&quot;https://www.charliecleveland.com/lawsuit/&quot;&gt;on Cleveland‚Äôs blog.&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;h2 class=&quot;wp-block-heading&quot;&gt;Krafton:&lt;/h2&gt;

&lt;blockquote class=&quot;wp-block-quote is-layout-flow wp-block-quote-is-layout-flow&quot;&gt;
&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;&lt;br&gt;To Our 12 Million Fellow Subnauts,&lt;/p&gt;



&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;‚Äî&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;Inevitable Leadership Change Driven by Project Abandonment‚ÄìDespite Holding 90% of Earnout for Themselves&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;



&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;First and foremost, we sincerely thank you for your continued support, passion, and unwavering dedication to Subnautica. We wish to provide clarity on the recent leadership changes at Unknown Worlds, a creative studio under KRAFTON.&lt;/p&gt;



&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Background of Leadership Change&amp;nbsp;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;



&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;KRAFTON deeply values Subnautica‚Äôs unique creativity and immersive world-building. To provide fans with even better gaming experiences, we acquired Unknown Worlds, fully committed to supporting Subnautica‚Äôs future success. We collaborated closely with the studio‚Äôs leadership, who were central to the creation of the original Subnautica, to foster the optimal environment for a successful Subnautica 2.&lt;/p&gt;



&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;Specifically, in addition to the initial $500 million purchase price, we allocated approximately 90% of the up to $250 million earn-out compensation to the three former executives, with the expectation that they would demonstrate leadership and active involvement in the development of Subnautica 2.&lt;/p&gt;



&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;However, regrettably, the former leadership abandoned the responsibilities entrusted to them. Subnautica 2 was originally planned for an Early Access launch in early 2024, but the timeline has since been significantly delayed. KRAFTON made multiple requests to Charlie and Max to resume their roles as Game Director and Technical Director, respectively, but both declined to do so. In particular, following the failure of Moonbreaker, KRAFTON asked Charlie to devote himself to the development of Subnautica 2. However, instead of participating in the game development, he chose to focus on a personal film project.&lt;/p&gt;



&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;KRAFTON believes that the absence of core leadership has resulted in repeated confusion in direction and significant delays in the overall project schedule.&lt;br&gt;The current Early Access version also falls short in terms of content volume.&lt;br&gt;We are deeply disappointed by the former leadership‚Äôs conduct, and above all, we feel a profound sense of betrayal by their failure to honor the trust placed in them by our fans.&lt;/p&gt;



&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;KRAFTON‚Äôs Full Support for the Dedicated Development Team&amp;nbsp;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;



&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;To uphold our commitment to provide you with the best possible gaming experience, we made the difficult yet necessary decision to change the executive leadership. Subnautica 2 has been and continues to be actively developed by a dedicated core team who share genuine passion, accountability, and commitment to the game. We deeply respect their expertise and creativity and will continue to provide full and unwavering support, enabling them to focus solely on delivering the exceptional game you deserve.&lt;/p&gt;



&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;KRAFTON‚Äôs Commitment to its Promises in Rewarding Employees&amp;nbsp;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;



&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;Additionally, KRAFTON has committed to fair and equitable compensation for all remaining Unknown Worlds employees who have continuously and tirelessly contributed to Subnautica 2‚Äôs development. We believe that the dedication and effort of this team are at the very heart of Subnautica‚Äôs ongoing evolution, and we reaffirm our commitment to provide the rewards they were promised.&lt;/p&gt;



&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;Fans will always remain at the center of every decision we make at KRAFTON. Moving forward, we promise transparent communication and continued efforts to sustainably develop and expand the beloved Subnautica universe.&lt;/p&gt;



&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Honoring your trust and expectations is a core tenet at KRAFTON. We are committed to repaying your patience with an even more refined and exceptional gaming experience.&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/blockquote&gt;

&lt;h2 class=&quot;wp-block-heading&quot;&gt;Cleveland&lt;/h2&gt;

&lt;blockquote class=&quot;wp-block-quote is-layout-flow wp-block-quote-is-layout-flow&quot;&gt;
&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;Hello everyone,&lt;/p&gt;



&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;It continues to be an explosive and surreal time for the Subnautica team and community. None of this is what we wanted. But we truly appreciate the amazing support we‚Äôve gotten from everyone. It means a lot to us, especially now.&lt;/p&gt;



&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;As&amp;nbsp;&lt;a href=&quot;https://www.charliecleveland.com/what-is-a-wave-but-a-thousand-drops/&quot;&gt;&lt;u&gt;I wrote last week&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;, we know in our souls that the game is ready for Early Access &amp;#8211; that‚Äôs just how we roll. And we‚Äôd like nothing more than for you to play it &lpar;game devs&amp;nbsp;&lt;strong&gt;live&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;nbsp;for this&rpar;. But it‚Äôs not currently under our control.&lt;/p&gt;



&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;We‚Äôve now filed a lawsuit against Krafton: the details should eventually become &lpar;at least mostly&rpar; public &amp;#8211; you all deserve the full story. Suing a multi-billion dollar company in a painful, public and possibly protracted way was certainly not on my bucket list. But this needs to be made right. Subnautica has been my life‚Äôs work and I would never willingly abandon it or the amazing team that has poured their hearts into it.&lt;/p&gt;



&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;As for the earnout, the idea that Max, Ted and I wanted to keep it all for ourselves is totally untrue. I‚Äôm in this industry because I love it, not for riches. Historically we‚Äôve always shared our profits with the team and did the same when we sold the studio. You can be damned sure we‚Äôll continue with the earnout/bonus as well. They deserve it for all their incredible work trying to get this great game into your hands.&lt;/p&gt;



&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;Stay tuned.&lt;/p&gt;



&lt;p class=&quot;has-text-align-none&quot;&gt;-Charlie&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/blockquote&gt;

## How It Works
This content is automatically updated using [blog-post-workflow](https://github.com/gautamkrishnar/blog-post-workflow), which fetches the latest content from various RSS feeds and updates this README.

## Usage for LinkedIn
The content cards above can be copied directly for use in LinkedIn posts. Each card includes:
- A headline
- A brief description
- A link to the full article
- Publication date

## Customize
To customize the feeds or layout, edit the `.github/workflows/content-aggregator.yml` file.
